<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the radio group package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> radio</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/radio-group&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>These are the key exports:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>

</span></div></pre>

<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code> when you need a vertical layout.</p>

<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="indicator" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Indicator<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#indicator"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Style the segmented control Indicator through the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">indicator</code> part.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;indicator&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for indicator */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="focused-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Focused State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#focused-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the radio input is focused, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-focus</code> attribute is added to the root
and label parts.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;radio&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-focus</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for radio focus state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;radio-label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-focus</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for radio label focus state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabled-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabled State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabled-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the radio is disabled, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-disabled</code> attribute is added to the root
and label parts.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;radio&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for radio disabled state */</span>

</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;radio-label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for radio label disabled state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="invalid-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Invalid State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#invalid-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the radio is invalid, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-invalid</code> attribute is added to the root and
label parts.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;radio&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-invalid</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for radio invalid state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;radio-label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-invalid</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for radio label invalid state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The radio group machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; label: string; indicator: string; item: (value: string) =&gt; string; itemLabel: (value: string) =&gt; string; itemControl: (value: string) =&gt; string; itemHiddenInput: (value: string) =&gt; string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the radio. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The controlled value of the radio group</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The initial value of the checked radio when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the value of the radio group.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The name of the input fields in the radio
(Useful for form submission).</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">form</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The associate form of the underlying input.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">If `true`, the radio group will be disabled</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">invalid</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">If `true`, the radio group is marked as invalid.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">required</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">If `true`, the radio group is marked as required.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">readOnly</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the radio group is read-only</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ValueChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called once a radio is checked</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;horizontal&quot; | &quot;vertical&quot;</code><span class="d_block">Orientation of the radio group</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;ltr&quot; | &quot;rtl&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The document&#x27;s text/writing direction.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The unique identifier of the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap Node | Document</code><span class="d_block">A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The radio group <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The current value of the radio group</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value: string) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to set the value of the radio group</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">clearValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Function to clear the value of the radio group</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">focus</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Function to focus the radio group</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getItemState</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(props: ItemProps) =&gt; ItemState</code><span class="d_block">Returns the state details of a radio input</span></li></ul>

small set.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/radio-group\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"SegmentedControl\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Syncs with `disabled` state of fieldset\n- Syncs with form `reset` events\n- Can programmatically set segmented control value\n- Can programmatically focus segmented control items\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the radio group package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"segmented-control/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the segmented control anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"segmented-control\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the radio group package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as radio from \"@zag-js/radio-group\"\n```\n\nThese are the key exports:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"segmented-control/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Setting the initial value\n\nUse the `defaultValue` property to set the segmented control's initial value.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(radio.machine, {\n  defaultValue: \"apple\",\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled segmented value\n\nUse `value` and `onValueChange` for controlled usage.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(radio.machine, {\n  value,\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    setValue(details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Programmatic value control\n\nUse the connected API when you need imperative updates.\n\n```jsx\napi.setValue(\"orange\")\napi.clearValue()\n```\n\n### Focusing from code\n\nUse `api.focus()` to move focus to the selected item (or first enabled item).\n\n```jsx\napi.focus()\n```\n\n### Listening for changes\n\nWhen the segmented control value changes, the `onValueChange` callback is\ninvoked.\n\n```jsx {2-7}\nconst service = useMachine(radio.machine, {\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string | null }\n    console.log(\"segmented control value is:\", details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Usage within forms\n\nTo use segmented control in forms, set `name` and render\n`api.getItemHiddenInputProps({ value })` for each item.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(radio.machine, {\n  name: \"fruits\",\n})\n```\n\n### Vertical orientation\n\nSet `orientation` when you need a vertical layout.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(radio.machine, {\n  orientation: \"vertical\",\n})\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n### Indicator\n\nStyle the segmented control Indicator through the `indicator` part.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"indicator\"] {\n  /* styles for indicator */\n}\n```\n\n### Focused State\n\nWhen the radio input is focused, the `data-focus` attribute is added to the root\nand label parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"radio\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for radio focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"radio-label\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for radio label focus state */\n}\n```\n\n### Disabled State\n\nWhen the radio is disabled, the `data-disabled` attribute is added to the root\nand label parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"radio\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for radio disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"radio-label\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for radio label disabled state */\n}\n```\n\n### Invalid State\n\nWhen the radio is invalid, the `data-invalid` attribute is added to the root and\nlabel parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"radio\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for radio invalid state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"radio-label\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for radio label invalid state */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe radio group machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"radio-group\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe radio group `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"radio-group\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"radio-group\"
